The Asilomar Conference Grounds, located in Pacific Grove, California, were constructed in 1913. They were added to the National Register of Historic Places on February 27, 1987, with the reference number 87000823. The architectural style of the Asilomar Conference Grounds is the Arts and Crafts movement.
The Asilomar Conference Grounds, located in Pacific Grove, California, were constructed in 1913 and are styled in the Arts and Crafts movement. They were added to the National Register of Historic Places on February 27, 1987, with the reference number 87000823.

The Asser Levy Public Baths were constructed in the year 1904 and are architecturally styled in the Romanesque Revival architecture. They are located on 23rd Street in Manhattan. The baths were added to the National Register of Historic Places on April 23, 1980, with the reference number 80002709.

The National Assembly of Azerbaijan is the legislative branch of the government in Azerbaijan. The head of government in Azerbaijan holds the title of Prime Minister. The capital city of Azerbaijan is Baku, and one of its notable landmarks is the Baku Turkish Martyrs Memorial. The memorial is made of red granite and white marble and was designed by Huseyn Butuner and Hilmi Gurer. It is dedicated to the Ottoman Army soldiers who were killed in the Battle of Baku.
The capital city of Azerbaijan is Baku. Azerbaijan is currently governed by a Prime Minister. The National Assembly is its legislative body. The Baku Turkish Martyrs Memorial, located in Azerbaijan, is dedicated to Ottoman Army soldiers killed in the Battle of Baku. It was designed by Huseyn Butuner and Hilmi Gunes and made of red granite and white marble.
